)@@G@@.       >>> BEGIN NYU LOCAL CODE >>>@[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         THE MD-KFA
)@@G@@EYIN ALLOWS THE CONSOLE OPERATOR TO ENTER A MESSAGE   @G@@@@.         OFFB
)@@G@@ UP TO 50 CHARACTERS THAT WILL BE DISPLAYED IMMEDIATELY     @G@@@@.     FC
)@@G@@    AFTER THE RUN CARD IN EACH PRINT FILE.  IF THE FIRST CHARACTER@G@@@@FD
)@@G@@.         IN THE KEYIN IS A '*', THE CURRENT MESSAGE WILL BE DELETED.   FE
)@@G@@@F@@@@.         IF THERE ARE NO CHARACTERS FOLLOWING THE MD, THE CURRENTFF
)@@G@@@D@@@@.         MESSAGE WILL BE DISPLAYED ON THE CONSOLE.   @[@@@@.     FG
)@@G@@@G@@@@.         THIS CODE CAME FROM THE UNIVERSITY OF MARYLAND, WHERE THFH
)@@G@@E     @^@@@@.         KEYIN IS 'AR'.@[@@@@.     @F@@@@ARPKT     EQUF    FI
)@@G@@  10,A2             . PACKET FOR COM$ & IOW$    @]@@@@ARBEGIN   . @F@@@@FJ
)@@G@@          L         A2,A0             . $P BUFFER ADDRESS TO A2   @F@@@@FK
)@@G@@          L,H2      A5,0,A2           . $P GET CHARACTER COUNT    @F@@@@FL
)@@G@@          JZ        A5,ARDISP         . $T CHARACTER COUNT ZERO?  @E@@@@FM
)@@G@@                                      . $A NO YES,ARDISP    @F@@@@      FN
)@@G@@    L,S1      A4,1,A2           . $P GET FIRST CHARACTER    @F@@@@      FO
)@@G@@    SZ        A0                . $P SET PRINT PACKET TO 0  @F@@@@      FP
)@@G@@    TNE,U     A4,'*'            . $T MESSAGE TO BE DELETED  @E@@@@      FQ
)@@G@@    J         ARDLT             . $A NO YES,ARDLT     @G@@@@          ANFR
)@@G@@,U      A5,1              . $P CONVERT CHARACTERS TO WORDS  @B@@@@      FS
)@@G@@    SZ        A4                .   @B@@@@          DI,U      A4,6      FT
)@@G@@        .   @G@@@@          TE,U      A4,8              . $T MORE THAN 4FU
)@@G@@8 CHARACTERS?     @E@@@@          J         ARDL1             . $A YES NFV
)@@G@@O,ARDL1     @F@@@@          L         A0,SPACES         . $P SPACE FILL FW
)@@G@@LAST WORD   @F@@@@          S,S3      A0,9,A2           . $P SPACE FILL FX
)@@G@@LAST WORD   @B@@@@          S,H2      A0,9,A2           .   @]@@@@ARDL1 FY
)@@G@@    . @E@@@@          A,U       A4,0201           . $P ADD SKIP COUNT   FZ
)@@G@@@G@@@@          L,U       A0,ARCSA+1        . $P GET ADDRESS OF CSA BUFFGA
)@@G@@ER + 1@F@@@@          LXI       A0,A4             . $P FORM PRINT$ PACKEGB
